        window.P.declare('glowMobileDoneBottonLabel', 'DONE');
      }
    });
  }
</script>

        These headphones are super comfortable and the sound quality is good. But the noise cancellation is useless. However, with the price point the value is good.

<span>No more airport noise!</span>
</span><div class="a-row a-spacing-none reviewByLine" data-hook="review-by-line"><span class="a-size-small a-color-tertiary review-date" data-hook="review-date">Reviewed in the United States on January 24, 2024</span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-mini a-grid-vertical-align a-grid-center"><span class="a-size-small a-color-tertiary" data-hook="format-strip-linkless">Color: Green</span></div><span class="cr-original-truncatable-content">
<div class="a-row a-spacing-small cr-truncated-content"><span class="review-text-sub-contents" data-hook="review-body">
  
    

    
      
        I'm generally a person who does not write reviews but I was so impressed with the noise cancellation ability of these headphones that I had to say something. I specifically purchased them for travelling. I hate the airport, I find it over stimulating, more so I hate the...
      

      
    
  
</span><span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="reviews:toggle-class:click" data-csa-c-func-deps="aui-da-reviews:toggle-class:click" data-csa-c-type="widget" data-reviews:toggle-class:click='{"cssClass":"aok-hidden","selector":"#customer_review-R2BARJ2Z3A18A5 .cr-truncated-content, #customer_review-R2BARJ2Z3A18A5 .cr-full-content"}'><a aria-label="Toggle full review text" class="a-link-normal a-nowrap a-text-normal" data-hook="redirect-see-more" href="/gp/aw/review/B0CJJJP1RD/R2BARJ2Z3A18A5/ref=cm_cr_arp_mb_rvw_tr?ie=UTF8"><span class="a-size-base cr-read-more">See more</span></a></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small cr-full-content aok-hidden"><span class="review-text-sub-contents" data-hook="review-body">
  
    

    
      
        I'm generally a person who does not write reviews but I was so impressed with the noise cancellation ability of these headphones that I had to say something. I specifically purchased them for travelling. I hate the airport, I find it over stimulating, more so I hate the noise of the airplane engines while flying, but these headphones have helped with both things tremendously.<br/><br/>I will say that they do not COMPLETELY block out sound, but the amount of noise they do let in is just enough to know when they are making announcements. For me, they let in the perfect amount of noise.

<div class="a-row" data-hook="genome-widget"><a class="a-profile" data-a-size="small" href="/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AEHI67ZYRBSI3DO3ULVIBLAWNANQ/ref=cm_cr_arp_mb_gw_tr?ie=UTF8"><div aria-hidden="true" class="a-profile-avatar-wrapper"><div class="a-profile-avatar"><img class="a-lazy-loaded" data-src="https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/S/amazon-avatars-global/default._CR0,0,1024,1024_SX110_.png" src="https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif"/><noscript><img src="https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/S/amazon-avatars-global/default._CR0,0,1024,1024_SX110_.png"/></noscript></div></div><div class="a-profile-content"><span class="a-profile-name">Eliot Simcoe</span></div></a></div><div class="a-section celwidget" id="customer_review-R9OYVHMZ1Y16X"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro a-grid-vertical-align a-grid-center"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star-small a-star-small-5 review-rating aok-align-center" data-hook="review-star-rating"><span class="a-icon-alt">5.0 out of 5 stars</span></i><span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold" data-hook="msrp-avp-badge-linkless">Verified Purchase</span></div><span class="a-size-base review-title-content a-color-base a-text-bold" data-hook="review-title">
<span>Super awesome headphones for the price</span>
</span><div class="a-row a-spacing-none reviewByLine" data-hook="review-by-line"><span class="a-size-small a-color-tertiary review-date" data-hook="review-date">Reviewed in the United States on September 2, 2021</span></div><span class="cr-original-truncatable-content">
<div class="a-row a-spacing-small cr-truncated-content"><span class="review-text-sub-contents" data-hook="review-body">
  
    

    
      
        I wear these when I'm running my serger to work and I'll run it for hours sometimes... My hearing was starting to get a little less than it once was and I'm only 33 at this rate I was looking at being deaf by 40 lol. So noise cancelling headphones is what I've been wearing...
      

      
    
  
</span><span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="reviews:toggle-class:click" data-csa-c-func-deps="aui-da-reviews:toggle-class:click" data-csa-c-type="widget" data-reviews:toggle-class:click='{"cssClass":"aok-hidden","selector":"#customer_review-R9OYVHMZ1Y16X .cr-truncated-content, #customer_review-R9OYVHMZ1Y16X .cr-full-content"}'><a aria-label="Toggle full review text" class="a-link-normal a-nowrap a-text-normal" data-hook="redirect-see-more" href="/gp/aw/review/B0CJJJP1RD/R9OYVHMZ1Y16X/ref=cm_cr_arp_mb_rvw_tr?ie=UTF8"><span class="a-size-base cr-read-more">See more</span></a></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small cr-full-content aok-hidden"><span class="review-text-sub-contents" data-hook="review-body">
  
    

    
      
        I wear these when I'm running my serger to work and I'll run it for hours sometimes... My hearing was starting to get a little less than it once was and I'm only 33 at this rate I was looking at being deaf by 40 lol. So noise cancelling headphones is what I've been wearing for a while. I had another pair but they had no speakers, strictly for working but I like to listen to music while I work or just have on some mindless something on my tablet that I'm watching here and there. These have great sound, they fit so nice... That's one thing I hated about the others was the tightness around my head... Not cool, have me a headache after a short while of wearing them, then it's like what's better a headache or going deaf??? So these were a perfect upgrade. Love them,y husband's jealous his PC doesn't have Bluetooth bc he wants a pair like mine for dota ^~^ he's go to have a corded pair... He's the techy one so it's kinda funny. Anyway I'd buy them again in an instant, the cushions on ears are amazing. Super nice. The pause button works awesome for YouTube and Netflix. I think I've used it for philo too, not sure though... I usually fast forward through commercial on TWD so idk...
      

      
    
  
</span></div></span>

<span class="a-end aok-hidden"></span></div>
</span>
</div><span class="cr-original-truncatable-content">
<div class="a-row a-spacing-small cr-truncated-content"><span class="review-text-sub-contents" data-hook="review-body">
  
    

    
      
         Stays connected to my phone unless I disconnect it. Then it drains the battery bc it's still trying to pair to something even though the power is off. Such a pain to manually pair and unpair it. Have to charge it so often even...
      

      
    
  
</span><span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="reviews:toggle-class:click" data-csa-c-func-deps="aui-da-reviews:toggle-class:click" data-csa-c-type="widget" data-reviews:toggle-class:click='{"cssClass":"aok-hidden","selector":"#customer_review-R26LTD6A5T529E .cr-truncated-content, #customer_review-R26LTD6A5T529E .cr-full-content"}'><a aria-label="Toggle full review text" class="a-link-normal a-nowrap a-text-normal" data-hook="redirect-see-more" href="/gp/aw/review/B0CJJJP1RD/R26LTD6A5T529E/ref=cm_cr_arp_mb_rvw_tr?ie=UTF8"><span class="a-size-base cr-read-more">See more</span></a></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small cr-full-content aok-hidden"><span class="review-text-sub-contents" data-hook="review-body">
  
    

    
      
         Stays connected to my phone unless I disconnect it. Then it drains the battery bc it's still trying to pair to something even though the power is off. Such a pain to manually pair and unpair it. Have to charge it so often even though I mainly only use them 10 mins 2x a day. I really don't understand all those reviews about the awesome battery life. And if I forget to unpair it, even if they are at a different location I can't hear any audio from my phone. Cute but poor quality. Fit is ok. In it's not adjustable and I have a small head, so I couldn't work out in these. Too loose.I haven't used them on a call, so I have no Idea . Music sounds fine. Frustrating in every other way though.
      

      
    
  
</span></div></span>
